            <h2>See the sites below to head in the right direction.</h2>
            <p>SSISurveys.com is the generic URL that Survey Sampling International, LLC  uses to host survey activity on all of our survey panels and survey activity from our partners. If you are a member of one of our branded survey panels or a member of one of our partners panels you may frequent the ssisurveys.com domain often and never really know it. If you are not an active member of any survey panels, please see the list of panels below to find the one that best fits you. </p>

            <h2>Who is Survey Sampling (SSI)?</h2>
            <p>Survey Sampling International (SSI) is a company which helps researchers listen to and access people's opinions. SSI is a member of the Council of American Survey Research Organizations (www.casro.org) and complies with research industry standards, best practices and relevant laws. SSI believes that legitimate research is a vital part of society because when people give their opinions, they can help shape, improve, and create products, services, programs, and policies that impact people, society and the world we live in.</p>

                <div class="def">
                    <h5>对话CEO：币必多-台湾第一家法币挖矿交易所</h5>
                </div>
                <div class="hov">
                    <!--<img src="https://c-img.18183.com/images/2018/08/13/c109e126e54af7eda5872e1ce60bcbb6.jpg@w_400,h_300,s_2" alt="对话CEO：币必多-台湾第一家法币挖矿交易所">-->
                    <div class="txt">
                        <h5>对话CEO：币必多-台湾第一家法币挖矿交易所</h5>
                        <p>前两月在厦门的一次meetup上，我们关注到台湾地区的创业家们正如火如荼地计划着进入区块链领域的各个细分市场。 作为现阶段区块链领域最为重要的流量入口之一，数字资产交易所是不容忽视的一方力量，因此我们有幸请到了即将上线的台湾第一家法币挖矿交易所币必多的CEO 杨俊书，来聊聊他对区块链</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </a>
        </li>
<li >
            <a href="http://finance.18183.com/201808/1153067.html" target="_blank" title="币圈血淋淋的“喊单”、伏击吸血、割韭菜">
                <div class="def">
                    <h5>币圈血淋淋的“喊单”、伏击吸血、割韭菜</h5>
                </div>
                <div class="hov">
                    <!--<img src="https://c-img.18183.com/images/2018/08/13/ae6ca8752e1931014243df6a582d6071.jpg@w_400,h_300,s_2" alt="币圈血淋淋的“喊单”、伏击吸血、割韭菜">-->
                    <div class="txt">
                        <h5>币圈血淋淋的“喊单”、伏击吸血、割韭菜</h5>
                        <p>这个周末，是市场非常惨的一个周末，除了做空的人、散户、大部分项目方、大部分市值团队，都损失惨重。币价已经跌破了很多老韭菜的心理支撑位，也跌破了很多币圈专家设置的短期支撑位，但是这还不是最惨的。因为现在价格下跌了，只是上一波投资的人获利收割完走人了。结果是数字货币的价值</p>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </a>
